<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ceder.html>ceder</a> (52227)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ceder.html>ceder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:ceder.html>ceder</a></i>, either indirectly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cedre</i> or directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cedrus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κέδρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kédros</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of unknown origin.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ceder.html>ceder</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ceders.html>ceders</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">cederen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ceder.html>cedertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***celluloid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a> (57893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Former trademark of <a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>Celluloid</a> Manufacturing Company
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/celluloid" class="extiw" title="w:celluloid"><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/celluloid" class="extiw" title="w:celluloid">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">celluloids</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of a variety of thermoplastics created from nitrocellulose and camphor, once used as photographic <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a>.
<ul><li><b>1894</b> June, Antonia Dickson, W. K. L. Dickson, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Century_Magazine/Volume_48/Issue_2/Edison%27s_Invention_of_the_Kineto-Phonograph:_Account_of_the_Invention" class="extiw" title="s:Century Magazine/Volume 48/Issue 2/Edison | s Invention of the Kineto-Phonograph: Account of the Invention">Edison's Invention of the Kineto-Phonograph: Account of the Invention</a></i>, article in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Century_Magazine" class="extiw" title="w:Century Magazine">Century Magazine</a></i>, Volume 48, Issue 2,
<dl><dd>Then followed some experiments with <a href = vnd.unilang:drums.html>drums</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> which sheets of sensitized <b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> drawn, the edges being pressed into a narrow <a href = vnd.unilang:slot.html>slot</a> in the surface, similar in construction to the old tin-foil phonograph.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1910</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_Leacock" class="extiw" title="w:Stephen Leacock">Stephen Leacock</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Conjurer%27s_Revenge" class="extiw" title="s:The Conjurer | s Revenge">The Conjurer's Revenge</a></i>, in <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Literary_Lapses" class="extiw" title="s:Literary Lapses">Literary Lapses</a></i>,
<dl><dd>"And will you now, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a>, take off your <b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b> collar and permit <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to burn it in the candle? Thank you, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a>. And will you allow <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to smash your spectacles for you with my hammer? Thank you."</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> often used attributively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The genre of cinema; <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a>.
<ul><li><b>2001</b> August 14, Riki Wilchins, <i>Gender on <b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b></i>, in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Advocate" class="extiw" title="w:The Advocate">The Advocate</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=B2MEAAAAMBAJamp;pg=PA26amp;dq=%22celluloid%22+-intitle:%22celluloid%22amp;hl=enamp;ei=ezPWTc-fEYb-vQPy1rGkBwamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;resnum=3amp;ved=0CD0Q6AEwAgv=onepageamp;q=%22celluloid%22%20-intitle%3A%22celluloid%22amp;f=false">page 26</a>.</li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b>,  Preston Whaley,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:blows.html>Blows</a> Like a Horn</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=eZefines2DcCamp;pg=PA82amp;dq=%22celluloid%22+-intitle:%22celluloid%22amp;hl=enamp;ei=ezPWTc-fEYb-vQPy1rGkBwamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;resnum=37amp;ved=0CO0BEOgBMCQv=onepageamp;q=%22celluloid%22%20-intitle%3A%22celluloid%22amp;f=false">[1]</a></sup>, page 20:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In particular, they set Kerouac and Ginsberg to the specifications of an emergent superficial form—<b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b> antiheroes—attractive to those in want of adventure and who would soon be reading <i>On the Road</i> (1957).</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestaande.html>bestaande</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> nitrocellulose <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>.a. <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruikt.html>gebruikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drager.html>drager</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fotografisch.html>fotografische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> cinematografische <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a>.</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a>, in contrast <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> video
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedraaid.html>gedraaid</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***celstraf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:celstraf.html>celstraf</a> (22891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cel.html>cel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:straf.html>straf</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">punishment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:celstraf.html>celstraf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:celstraffen.html>celstraffen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:celstraf.html>celstrafje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>prison sentence, jail term</li></ol>

***censureren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:censureren.html>censureren</a> (52225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">censurer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:censureren.html>censureren</a></strong>

***center.html

<p><b>center</b>
</p>
<ol><li>(<i><a href = vnd.unilang:verenigde.html>Verenigde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staten.html>Staten</a></i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:centrum.html>centrum</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:midden.html>midden</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:centerfold.html>centerfold</a> (45720)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:centurion.html>centurion</a> (26299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">centuriō, centuriōnis</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">centum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a hundred</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:centurion.html>centurion</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:centurions.html>centurions</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An officer of the ancient Roman army, in command of a century of <a href = vnd.unilang:soldiers.html>soldiers</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cricket</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A player who <a href = vnd.unilang:scores.html>scores</a> a century.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pilot in the United States Navy who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> performed 100 night <a href = vnd.unilang:landings.html>landings</a> on an aircraft carrier.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ceremonie.html>ceremonie</a> (5059)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cerimonie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:ceremonie.html>ceremonie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caerimonia</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caeremonia</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> often <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cerimonia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sacredness, reverence, a sacred rite</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cha.html>cha</a> (52224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">kweman</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">chuman</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kwemaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kommen.html>kommen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">come</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">koma</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌵𐌹𐌼𐌰𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qiman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chanson.html>chanson</a> (118823)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:chanson.html>chanson</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:chanson.html>chanson</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">chançon</i>, inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cantiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:chanson.html>chanson</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:chanson.html>chansons</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:chanson.html>chansonnetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chanson.html>chanson</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">French, lyric-driven song</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***chanteren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:chanteren.html>chanteren</a> (9283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">chanter</i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:chanteren.html>chanteren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to extort money, to blackmail</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
